Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

This is introduced by this commit 



<span class="line"><!---->This is introduced by this commit <!----></span>





21ae413b543e464de8646164d05325f2f86656f7

Note that this UAF doesn't need any flag or user interactions, so I think it should be a critical issue.



<span class="line"><!---->Note that this UAF doesn't need any flag or user interactions, so I think it should be a critical issue.<!----></span>

In this commit

21ae413b543e464de8646164d05325f2f86656f7



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/21ae413b543e464de8646164d05325f2f86656f7"><!---->21ae413b543e464de8646164d05325f2f86656f7<!----></a>





, a new check is added to function `PaymentManifestDownloader::InitiateDownload(`[1], the `csp_checker_`(1). If this `csp_checker_` is null, then it will call `RespondWithError`[2], this will run callback directly.



<span class="line"><!---->, a new check is added to function `PaymentManifestDownloader::InitiateDownload(`[1], the `csp_checker_`(1). If this `csp_checker_` is null, then it will call `RespondWithError`[2], this will run callback directly.<!----></span>

For this issue, when we call function `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestParsed`[3], it will call `DownloadWebAppManifest`(2), and pass the callback `OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded`(3). `DownloadWebAppManifest` will call `PaymentManifestDownloader::InitiateDownload`[1], so if `csp_checker_` is null, `OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded` will run immediately.



<span class="line"><!---->For this issue, when we call function `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestParsed`[3], it will call `DownloadWebAppManifest`(2), and pass the callback `OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded`(3). `DownloadWebAppManifest` will call `PaymentManifestDownloader::InitiateDownload`[1], so if `csp_checker_` is null, `OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded` will run immediately.<!----></span>



<br>

In function `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded`[4], if the `content`(4) is empty(`RespondWithError` will run ``InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded` with an empty `content`(5)), `FinishCrawlingPaymentAppsIfReady()` will be called, which will run `finished_using_resources_` callback.



<span class="line"><!---->In function `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded`[4], if the `content`(4) is empty(`RespondWithError` will run ``InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded` with an empty `content`(5)), `FinishCrawlingPaymentAppsIfReady()` will be called, which will run `finished_using_resources_` callback.<!----></span>

<br>



<br>





`finished_using_resources_` callback is initialized in function `OnPaymentAppsVerified`[5]. The `finished_using_resources_` is assigned as `&SelfDeletingServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder::OnPaymentAppsCrawlerFinishedUsingResources`[6]. 



<span class="line"><!---->`finished_using_resources_` callback is initialized in function `OnPaymentAppsVerified`[5]. The `finished_using_resources_` is assigned as `&amp;SelfDeletingServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder::OnPaymentAppsCrawlerFinishedUsingResources`[6]. <!----></span>



<br>





And `SelfDeletingServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder::OnPaymentAppsCrawlerFinishedUsingResources` will reset the `crawler_` directly! This `crawler_` is the class where we run `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestParsed`[3]. So when the code continue running, it will use the freed memory(6).



<span class="line"><!---->And `SelfDeletingServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder::OnPaymentAppsCrawlerFinishedUsingResources` will reset the `crawler_` directly! This `crawler_` is the class where we run `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestParsed`[3]. So when the code continue running, it will use the freed memory(6).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```[5]

2. POC



<span class="line"><!---->2. POC<!----></span>



<br>





`csp_checker_` is weakPtr in `PaymentManifestDownloader`, and is owned by `ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder`, `ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder` is bound to `content::DocumentUserData`, so we can refresh the frame to free it. You can see the poc.html and test.html for more info.



<span class="line"><!---->`csp_checker_` is weakPtr in `PaymentManifestDownloader`, and is owned by `ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder`, `ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder` is bound to `content::DocumentUserData`, so we can refresh the frame to free it. You can see the poc.html and test.html for more info.<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





class ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder



<span class="line"><!---->class ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder<!----></span>



<br>





    : public content::DocumentUserData<ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder> {



<span class="line"><!---->    : public content::DocumentUserData&lt;ServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder&gt; {<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

3. Supplement 



<span class="line"><!---->3. Supplement <!----></span>



<br>





Besides, `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestDownloaded`[8] has a similar logic with `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded`[4], which could also call `FinishCrawlingPaymentAppsIfReady()`. So it could also be used to trigger this UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->Besides, `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestDownloaded`[8] has a similar logic with `InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentWebAppManifestDownloaded`[4], which could also call `FinishCrawlingPaymentAppsIfReady()`. So it could also be used to trigger this UAF.<!----></span>



<br>

                       because of the empty `contents`.



<span class="line"><!---->                       because of the empty `contents`.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->    1.3) InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::FinishCrawlingPaymentAppsIfReady() invokes<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->                       the `finished_using_resouces_` callback.<!----></span>

                       OnPaymentAppsCrawlerFinishedUsingResources().



<span class="line"><!---->                       OnPaymentAppsCrawlerFinishedUsingResources().<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->                      the InstallablePaymentAppCrawler via `crawler_.reset()` statement.<!----></span>

#c17



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c17"><!---->#c17<!----></a>





 makes sense to me. InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestParsed has that call to handle the case where |default_applications| is empty or none of them are valid (e.g., blocked, etc), but it doesn't expect a synchronous deletion of its own object.



<span class="line"><!----> makes sense to me. InstallablePaymentAppCrawler::OnPaymentMethodManifestParsed has that call to handle the case where |default_applications| is empty or none of them are valid (e.g., blocked, etc), but it doesn't expect a synchronous deletion of its own object.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The overall lifecycle of SelfDeletingServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder seems quite dangerous and something we should look at in the future, but hopefully we can get a targeted fix in for this case.



<span class="line"><!---->The overall lifecycle of SelfDeletingServiceWorkerPaymentAppFinder seems quite dangerous and something we should look at in the future, but hopefully we can get a targeted fix in for this case.<!----></span>

The reason for difficulty to reproduce this bug is due to `PaymentManifestDownloader::csp_checker_` having to be reset to null after PaymentManifestDownloader::DownloaderPaymentMethodManifest(), but before PaymentManifestDownloader::DownloadWebAppManifest(). That is a short period of time.



<span class="line"><!---->The reason for difficulty to reproduce this bug is due to `PaymentManifestDownloader::csp_checker_` having to be reset to null after PaymentManifestDownloader::DownloaderPaymentMethodManifest(), but before PaymentManifestDownloader::DownloadWebAppManifest(). That is a short period of time.<!----></span>

Bug: 1366806

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

Congratulations, Weipeng Jiang! The VRP Panel has decided to award you $30,000 + $7,000 renderer RCE bonus + $1,000 bisect bonus for a total of $38,000 for this report. Really neat bug, great find, and excellent report! Thank you for your efforts in discovering and reporting this issue to us -- great work!

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
